   13   static double rt_powd_snf(double u0, double u1);
   14   
   15   // Function Definitions
   16   
   17   //
   18   // Arguments    : double u0
   19   //                double u1
   20   // Return Type  : double
   21   //
   22   static double rt_powd_snf(double u0, double u1)
   23   {
   24     double y;
   25     double d0;
   26     double d1;
   27     if (rtIsNaN(u0) || rtIsNaN(u1)) {
   28       y = rtNaN;
   29     } else {
   30       d0 = std::abs(u0);
   31       d1 = std::abs(u1);
   32       if (rtIsInf(u1)) {
   33         if (d0 == 1.0) {
   34           y = rtNaN;
   35         } else if (d0 > 1.0) {
   36           if (u1 > 0.0) {
   37             y = rtInf;
   38           } else {
   39             y = 0.0;
   40           }
   41         } else if (u1 > 0.0) {
   42           y = 0.0;
   43         } else {
   44           y = rtInf;
   45         }
   46       } else if (d1 == 0.0) {
   47         y = 1.0;
   48       } else if (d1 == 1.0) {
   49         if (u1 > 0.0) {
   50           y = u0;
   51         } else {
   52           y = 1.0 / u0;
   53         }
   54       } else if (u1 == 2.0) {
   55         y = u0 * u0;
   56       } else if ((u1 == 0.5) && (u0 >= 0.0)) {
   57         y = std::sqrt(u0);
   58       } else if ((u0 < 0.0) && (u1 > std::floor(u1))) {
   59         y = rtNaN;
   60       } else {
   61         y = pow(u0, u1);
   62       }
   63     }
   64   
   65     return y;
   66   }

 1339     double fxb_a;
 1340     double gxb_a;
 1341     double hxb_a;
 1342     double ixb_a;

 1344     double kxb_a;
 1345     double lxb_a;
 1346     double mxb_a;
 1347     double nxb_a;
 1348     double oxb_a;
 1349     double pxb_a;
 1350     double qxb_a;
 1351     double rxb_a;
 1352     double sxb_a;
 1353     double txb_a;
 1354     double uxb_a;
 1355     double vxb_a;
 1356     double wxb_a;
 1357     double xxb_a;
 1358     double yxb_a;
 1359     double ayb_a;
 1360     double byb_a;
 1361     double cyb_a;
 1362     double dyb_a;
 1363     double eyb_a;
 1364   
 1365     // p_x_p_Lgh_baru is 1-by-5
 1366     b_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1367     c_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1368     d_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1369     e_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1370     f_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1371     g_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1372     h_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1373     i_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1374     j_a = (pos_ob_x - s) * ((vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::
 1375       sin(epsi)) + (ey - pos_ob_y) * ((yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) +
 1376       xp_dot * std::sin(epsi));
 1377     k_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1378     l_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1379     m_a = (vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1380     n_a = (yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) + xp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1381     o_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1382     p_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1383     q_a = (vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1384     r_a = (yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) + xp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1385     s_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1386     t_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1387     u_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1388     v_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1389     w_a = (pos_ob_x - s) * ((vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::
 1390       sin(epsi)) + (ey - pos_ob_y) * ((yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) +
 1391       xp_dot * std::sin(epsi));
 1392     x_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1393     y_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1394     ab_a = (vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1395     bb_a = (yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) + xp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1396     cb_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1397     db_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1398     eb_a = (vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1399     fb_a = (yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) + xp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1400     gb_a = (pos_ob_x - s) * ((vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::
 1401       sin(epsi)) + (ey - pos_ob_y) * ((yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) +
 1402       xp_dot * std::sin(epsi));
 1403     hb_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1404     ib_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1405     jb_a = (vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1406     kb_a = (yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) + xp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1407     lb_a = pos_ob_x - s;
 1408     mb_a = ey - pos_ob_y;
 1409     nb_a = (vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1410     ob_a = (yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) + xp_dot * std::sin(epsi);
 1411     pb_a = (pos_ob_x - s) * ((vel_ob_x - xp_dot * std::cos(epsi)) + yp_dot * std::
 1412       sin(epsi)) + (ey - pos_ob_y) * ((yp_dot * std::cos(epsi) - vel_ob_y) +
 1413       xp_dot * std::sin(epsi));
 1414     qb_a = pos_ob_x - s;
